```
     0x4810 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 236*
     0x4815 [0x01] GOTO 0x485D
     0x4818 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 2*) GOTO 0x4828
     0x4820 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 412*
     0x4825 [0x01] GOTO 0x485D
     0x4828 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 3*) GOTO 0x483D
     0x4830 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 403*
     0x4835 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[19] = 0*
     0x483A [0x01] GOTO 0x485D
     0x483D [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 4*) GOTO 0x484D
     0x4845 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 454*
     0x484A [0x01] GOTO 0x485D
     0x484D [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 5*) GOTO 0x485D
     0x4855 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 455*
     0x485A [0x01] GOTO 0x485D
     0x485D [0x1B] RETURN
```
